<!--
This file was generated by the NES PWAA project.

=================================
# ACE ATTORNEY - PHOENIX WRIGHT #
#        DIALOG SCRIPTS         #
=================================

Description:
  This file contain all the dialogs of the first Ace Attorney game
  but formatted to be use as text for my 'NES PWAA' project.
  The format of this document is similar to the HTML syntax (but worse)
  Quick description about the format:
  - DIALOGS are written as normal, just like in a plain text document.
    All control characters are removed from the text (including new line)
  - SPECIAL CHARACTERS are written with tag, example: <special_char:arg1,arg2,...>
    Inside the tag, the character name is present before the colon and after it are arguments.
    Each argument is separated by a comma. There effects depend on the special character.
  - COMMENTS are like HTML, example : <!-- This is a comment -->
<!--                                                          ^
    Note the open comment the line before, because of this up there, the comment above closed.
    You cannot really put comments into comments without closing the previous one (because i'm lazy and it is enough for now).


/!\ /!\ /!\ TODO /!\ /!\ /!\
--------------------------
|        CHAPTERS        |
--------------------------
| lines : chapter name
| (tips: use ctrl-f to jump to the corresponding title)
| - - - - - - - - - - - - - - - 
/!\ /!\ /!\ TODO /!\ /!\ /!\
-->
